-----------------

Day 1:
	Gwalior - Varanasi (Train - 950(approx +-50))
Day 2:
	Rs. 100 Kuch bahar ka kha liya(Train ya Station)
	Reached Varanasi (Hotel - 800 each(2-3 in one room))
			 (Food - 400 (chaat+evening snacks+dinner))
			 (Rs. 200 Extra + auto/Taxi)
			 (Boat - 100-300(depending on crowd))
Day 3:
	(Day 2 in Varanasi)
	Rs. 50-100 (breakfast)
	Prasad (shradha anusar)
	Varanasi - New Jalpaiguri (Train - 950)
	food (Rs. 500 (lunch + dinner + evening snacks))
Day 4:
	Toy Train (Rs. 1600)
	Reach Darjeeling (Hotel - 800 each)
			 (Food - 600-700 each(Veg in darjeeling is expensive)
			 (Taxi - 100)
			 (200 Extra)
Day 5:
	Day 2 in darjeeling
		(Hotel - 800)
		(Food - 600)
		(Taxi/Renting bike - 300(aaj ghumege))
		(200 Extra)
Day 6:
	Day 3 in darjeeling
		(Hotel Checkout)
		(Taxi - 600 each to reach New Jalpaiguri)
	New Jalpaiguri - Varanasi (950)
	food( 400)
Day 7:
	Varanasi - Gwalior (950)
	food (400)

[14/01/24, 20:58:08] Yash Agrawal Mits: Just a cautionary advice to all those who belong to the Content writing club:

We all know ki tum log majority time ChatGPT ka use karte ho, content share karne ke liye.

Main bas apna kahoonga ki main jab se is club mein hoon aur mere saath Wale log, ham logo ne kabhi kisi AI ya website ki help nahi li, content writing ke liye.
Hamne hamesha original content hi banaya hai aur usse hame fayda hi hua hai, language ki proficiency mei aur apne thoughts express karne mei.

To advise yahi hai ki try Karo, khud se sochke content banao, isse tumhe hi fayda hoga. Baaki ye college ka assignment to hai nahi ki tumhe poora karna hai to kisi digital tool se karlo.

Try to bring original content, made by you. Haa reference le sakte ho, but...... Khair, I hope you understand what I mean to say
